***пробегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробега́ть</a> (7444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробежать.html>пробежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run past, to run through</li>
<li>to run a certain distance or for some time</li>
<li>to skim, to scan, to look through</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробе́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probégatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend some time running</li></ol>

***пробежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробежать.html>пробежа́ть</a> (4186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробежать.html>пробежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run past, to run through</li>
<li>to run a certain distance or for some time</li>
<li>to skim, to scan, to look through</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробежка.html>пробе́жка</a> (21782)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробега́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probegátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́вший</a> (11409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́вший</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.

<ol><li>to punch out

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probivátʹ</b> bilét</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to punch/cancel a ticket</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pierce, to go <i>(through)</i></li>
<li>to break <i>(through)</i>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press <i>(for)</i>, to push <i>(for)</i>, to struggle <i>(for)</i>, to win, to bring off, to put across

</p>
<ol><li>to fight/force/make one's way through, to break/win/strike through

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>трудо́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s trudóm <b>probivátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to struggle through</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shoot, to show, to push up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of plants</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***пробирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробирать.html>пробира́ть</a> (23231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробирать.html>пробира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пробра́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel strong coldness of the air or wind</li>
<li>to scold</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробираться.html>пробира́ться</a> (4593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробираться.html>пробира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробраться.html>пробра́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to make one's way, to thread one's way, to pick one's way, to edge through

***пробить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a> (3912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*probiti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pro-</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*biti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to punch out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыру́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> dyrú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make/punch/pierce a hole</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> bilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to punch/cancel a ticket</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pierce, to go <i>(through)</i></li>
<li>to break <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> stenu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">break through a wall</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make <i>(a road, a tunnel)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туннель.html>тунне́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> tunnɛ́lʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a tunnel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break a way</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to issue a check/chit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay to the cashier</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press <i>(for)</i>, to push <i>(for)</i>, to struggle <i>(for)</i>, to win, to bring off, to put across
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрешение.html>разреше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> razrešénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to struggle to obtain permission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снижение.html>сниже́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:налог.html>нало́гов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> snižénije nalógov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to push for taxes to be reduced</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:льгота.html>льго́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> sebé lʹgótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win a (hard-to-get) benefit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правительство.html>прави́тельство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спешно.html>спе́шно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поправка.html>попра́вки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ну</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pravítelʹstvo spéšno <b>probílo</b> poprávki k zakónu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the cabinet rammed/railroaded the amendments to the law</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strike, to sound
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ли</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>про́били</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">časý <b>probíli</b>/<b>próbili</b> pjatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the clock struck five</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробиться.html>проби́ться</a> (5806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиться.html>проби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fight/force/make one's way through, to break/win/strike through</li>
<li><i>(of plants)</i> to shoot, to show, to push up</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>би́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***пробка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробка.html>про́бка</a> (4928)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробка.html>про́бка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próbka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробка.html>про́бки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробка.html>про́бки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробка.html>про́бок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plug</li>
<li>cork</li>
<li>congestion</li>
<li>traffic jam</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fuse (<i>device preventing overloading of a circuit</i>)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a> (14707)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>про́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próbnyj</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробовавший.html>про́бовавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próbovavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробовать.html>про́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próbovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробовавший.html>про́бовавший</a></b>

***пробовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробовать.html>про́бовать</a> (2611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>про́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">próba</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Probe</i>, from Middle Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">proba</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">probō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pro-bhwo-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">being in front</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from *pro-, a variant of the base *per-, + the base *bhu- (to be).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробовать.html>про́бовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próbovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попробовать.html>попро́бовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to test, to attempt, to try</li>
<li>to taste (to sample the flavor of something), to feel</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>parting <i>(of hair)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prjamój <b>probór</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>parting</b> in the middle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>но́сит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:коса.html>косо́й</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́р</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On nósit vólosy na prjamój (kosój) <b>probór</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">His hair is parted in the middle (at one side).</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdélatʹ (sebé) <b>probór</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to part one's hair</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пробраться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробраться.html>пробра́ться</a> (6785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">прабрацца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prabracca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">пробратися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probratysja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробраться.html>пробра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробираться.html>пробира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make one's way, to thread one's way, to pick one's way, to edge through
